Method: 基于分类器的审计框架：以人类语音为基准，训练分类器检测特定音系模式（如ATR元音和谐），然后将训练好的分类器迁移到TTS合成语音上，对比分类器预测标签与转录标签的一致性，评估TTS系统对音系对比的忠实度。

Result: 1) 基于人类语音训练的分类器迁移到合成语音后性能损失极小；2) Meta的MMS TTS中，1/3的[+ATR]中元音被实现为[-ATR]；3) 词级别上，分类器预测的ATR标签比转录标签更准确地反映和谐模式；4) 该框架可推广到其他具有可测量声学线索的音系对比。

Conclusion: 提出的忠实度审计框架能够有效检测TTS系统在音系层面的失败，发现标准评估无法揭示的系统性偏差，为任务特定诊断提供了通用方法。

Abstract: Neural TTS systems can sound natural across languages, but naturalness does not guarantee the preservation of sound contrasts that distinguish words from their grammatical forms. Standard metrics like MOS do not test for this. We propose a classifier-based framework that audits TTS output against language-specific phonological patterns using human speech as a benchmark. Testing Assamese advanced tongue root (ATR) vowel harmony with Meta's MMS TTS, we show that a classifier trained on human speech transfers to synthesized speech with minimal loss. The faithfulness audit reveals that [+ATR] mid vowels are realized as [-ATR] in 1/3 tokens despite an underlying [+ATR] specification, a bias absent in human speech. At the word level, predicted ATR labels classify harmony more accurately than transcription labels, indicating a gap between intended and produced phonology. The framework offers task-specific diagnostics and generalizes to other phonological contrasts with measurable acoustic cues.

### [162] [Object Aligner: A Configurable JSON Schema Similarity Score for Graphs, Applied to LLM Prompt Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01972)
*Jan Drchal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Object Aligner (OA) 是一个开源 Python 库，通过递归树对齐（无序集合用匈牙利算法，有序序列用序列对齐）和 JSON Schema 扩展配置，实现 JSON 对象的确定性评分；其核心贡献是**引用对齐**（referential alignment），通过 Weisfeiler-Leman 颜色细化近似推断标识符双射，使分数对重标号不变，并支持排序敏感场景和免费修复建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估 LLM 生成的 JSON 与黄金参考的匹配度的方法各有缺陷：精确匹配过于脆弱、文本相似度忽略结构、LLM 裁判昂贵且非确定性；此外，复杂结构化数据（图/超图）中的任意标识符引用打破了传统树相似度度量的假设。

Method: 提出 Object Aligner：(1) 通过 JSON Schema 扩展声明式配置，无需写代码；(2) 递归对齐两棵 JSON 树，无序集合用匈牙利算法、有序序列用序列对齐；(3) 核心创新**引用对齐**，用 Weisfeiler-Leman 颜色细化近似求解标识符双射（图同构的近似），使评分对重标号不变；(4) 同时输出排序后的修复建议。

Result: 作为 GEPA 提示优化器中的奖励函数时，Object Aligner 在所有数据集上表现持平或更好。

Conclusion: Object Aligner 提供了一种确定性、可配置、结构感知的 JSON 匹配度评分方案，解决了引用重标号下的对齐问题，并能在无额外成本下生成修复建议。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are often asked to produce JSON conforming to a fixed schema, powering information extraction, tool calling, agentic planning, and knowledge-graph construction. Measuring how closely an output matches a gold reference is essential yet surprisingly hard: exact match is brittle, text similarity ignores structure, and an LLM judge is expensive, opaque, and non-deterministic. We address this with Object Aligner (OA), an open-source Python library that scores two JSON objects deterministically by recursively aligning their trees (the Hungarian algorithm for unordered collections, sequence alignment for ordered ones) and awarding partial credit at the granularity the schema declares. The Object Aligner is configured entirely through a set of JSON Schema extensions, so adapting it to a new task involves annotating a schema rather than writing code. Complex structured data, however, are rarely flat trees: records may form graphs or hypergraphs keyed by arbitrary identifiers, breaking the assumptions of prior similarity metrics. Our central contribution, referential alignment, closes this gap by inferring a bijection between gold and candidate identifiers and scoring every reference through it, so the score is invariant to relabeling. Since recovering this bijection exactly is graph isomorphism, the Object Aligner approximates it with Weisfeiler-Leman color refinement. An order-sensitive sequence regime targets ranking and planning. Since the same alignment localizes every mismatch, the Object Aligner emits ranked repair suggestions at no extra cost. Used as a reward inside the GEPA prompt optimizer, Object Aligner helps or stays neutral across all datasets.

</details>

Method: 从普通话自然口语语料库中提取7470个单音节CV词，使用语境化嵌入作为预测变量，通过类型级和词例级排列基线评估CEs对词长预测的显著性与精度，并检验预测时长能否将归一化f0轮廓反变换回毫秒时间尺度。

Abstract: Time-normalized f0 contours of Mandarin words in conversational speech have been shown to be predictable in part from their contextualized embeddings (CEs). The present study investigates whether CEs also predict spoken word duration for 7470 tokens of Mandarin monosyllabic CV words extracted from a Mandarin corpus of spontaneous speech. We show that CEs indeed are predictive for duration, above chance level, not only at the type level, but also at the level of individual tokens, as indicated by the results obtained with the type-wise and token-wise permutation baselines. We also show that the predicted durations are sufficiently precise to back-transform predicted f0 contours in [0,1] normalized time to contours on the ms time scale. The resulting predicted contours approximate empirical contours and also outperform a permutation baseline.

### [164] [EduArt: An educational-level benchmark for evaluating art history knowledge in large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02007)
*Gianmarco Spinaci,Lukas Klic,Giovanni Colavizza*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍EduArt，一个由871道人工出题构成的艺术史知识多模态基准，涵盖两种语言和七种题型。评估12个模型后发现：选择题性能饱和（6个模型接近天花板），但开放完成题正确率骤降至23.9%（Claude Opus 4.6），错误识别题仅6.2%（Claude Sonnet 4.6）。格式是准确率的强预测因子，动机条件（要求书面论证）对准确率有负向影响。研究表明艺术史知识与知识运用能力是分离的，单一格式基准会高估模型能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在通用基准上得分接近天花板，但难以揭示其在单一学科内的真实行为。已有的艺术评估依赖合成问题且很少报告项目层面的属性，需一个更严谨、基于真实教育材料的多模态艺术史基准。

Method: 构建EduArt基准（871道人工出题，来自意大利中学和美国AP艺术史考试，涵盖2种语言、7种格式）。对12个模型（6个系列）在默认仅答案条件和动机条件（需书面论证）下评估，使用经典测试理论分析心理测量属性，并用Logistic回归分离格式、语言、图像存在和模型的影响。

Result: 基准具有良好的心理测量属性（平均区分度0.514，82.3%为良好区分项）。选择题性能饱和（6个模型近天花板），但开放完成题仅23.9%（Claude Opus 4.6），错误识别题仅6.2%（Claude Sonnet 4.6）。格式是准确率的强独立预测因子，动机条件对准确率有负向影响且呈家族依赖方向。

Conclusion: 艺术史知识与知识运用能力是分离的两种能力，单一格式基准会高估模型在真实任务中的表现。绘制能力剖面图是负责任地将多模态LLM用于艺术史研究的先决条件，因为该领域任务要求生成和操作内容，而非从固定选项中挑选。

Abstract: Large language models now score near ceiling on general benchmarks, but these aggregate measures reveal little about how models behave within single disciplines. Existing art-focused evaluations rely on synthetic questions and rarely report item-level properties. This paper introduces EduArt, an educational-level benchmark for art-historical knowledge and visual reasoning in multimodal LLMs. EduArt comprises 871 human-authored questions from Italian secondary-school exercises and US Advanced Placement Art History exams, spanning two languages and seven formats from multiple choice to in-text word placement and error identification. Twelve models from six provider families were evaluated under a default answer-only condition and a motivation condition requiring written justification, and characterized using Classical Test Theory and a logistic regression isolating the effects of format, language, image presence, and model. The benchmark showed strong psychometric properties (mean discrimination 0.514, 82.3 percent good discriminators), while multiple-choice accuracy saturated near ceiling for six models, showing recognition formats alone cannot distinguish frontier models. Format was a strong independent predictor of accuracy: models exceeding 94 percent on multiple choice fell to 23.9 percent on open completion (Claude Opus 4.6) and 6.2 percent on error identification (Claude Sonnet 4.6). The motivation condition changed accuracy in a predominantly negative, family-dependent direction. These dissociations indicate that art-historical knowledge and the ability to deploy it are distinct capabilities, and that single-format benchmarks overestimate what models can reliably do. Mapping this capability profile is a precondition for responsible use of multimodal LLMs in art-historical scholarship, where tasks demand producing and manipulating content rather than selecting from fixed options.

### [165] [OpenSafeIntent: Evaluating Intent-Calibrated Safe Completion Across Dual-Use Prompt Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02047)
*Rheeya Uppaal,Seungwoo Lyu,Selina Sung,Junjie Hu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Safe completion requires models to provide useful assistance without enabling harm, but this behavior is difficult to evaluate with isolated prompts. We introduce OpenSafeIntent, a benchmark of controlled prompt-sets that vary intent while holding the underlying task fixed. Each datapoint contains benign, dual-use, and malicious variants of the same task. This design lets us evaluate whether models calibrate assistance across intent shifts, rather than merely appearing safe on average. Across a broad model suite, we find that prompt-level safety hides important failures: models often fail to remain safe across matched intent variants, dual-use behavior is brittle under paraphrase, high-level answers on risky topics are not reliably safe, and responses that reframe ambiguous requests into safer tasks are substantially less likely to cross the safety boundary. Our results suggest that safe completion should be evaluated as intent-calibrated behavior over controlled task variants, not as a single safety-helpfulness tradeoff over independent prompts.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型越来越多地被部署在情绪支持和危机干预场景中，但其跨语言能力在这些情境下尚未得到充分探索。现有基准侧重于多语言性能，很少考察中低资源语言中的危机相关同理心和文化扎根性。

Method: 构建SPLIT基准，包含500个提示，覆盖压力、恐慌、孤独、内部流离失所和紧张五个类别。从同理心准确性、语言自然度、上下文与文化扎根性三个维度评估三个技术多样的LLM，并探索LLM-as-a-jury范式的可靠性。

Result: Gemini-2.5-Flash和LLaMA-3.3-70B-Instruct在切换到乌克兰语时性能下降，DeepSeek-V3保持相对稳定。人类与AI评估者在同理心和自然度上弱一致，但在文化扎根性上存在分歧。

Conclusion: 生成乌克兰语文本不等同于生成乌克兰语情绪支持。研究结果有助于未来开发更具文化针对性的基准设计，并强调以人为中心的评估的重要性。

Abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly deployed in emotional-support contexts and crisis-related situations. Nevertheless, their cross-lingual abilities in these circumstances remain underexplored. Existing benchmarks emphasize multilingual performance but rarely examine crisis-related empathy and cultural grounding in low-to-mid-resource languages. We introduce SPLIT, a 500-prompt benchmark designed to evaluate LLM consistency in generating emotionally grounded responses across five categories: Stress, Panic, Loneliness, Internal Displacement, and Tension. We evaluate three technically diverse LLMs across three dimensions: Empathetic Accuracy, Linguistic Naturalness, and Contextual & Cultural Grounding. The framework aims to assess and compare the quality of LLM responses in both English and Ukrainian languages, as well as to explore the reliability of the LLM-as-a-jury paradigm. Our findings reveal that Gemini-2.5-Flash and LLaMA-3.3-70B-Instruct degrade when transitioning to Ukrainian, while DeepSeek-V3 remains comparatively stable within our benchmark. We additionally find that human and AI evaluators agree weakly on empathy and naturalness but diverge on cultural grounding. We further argue that producing Ukrainian text is not equivalent to producing Ukrainian emotional support. Our findings may assist in the future development of more culturally tailored benchmark designs, as well as encourage a stronger emphasis on human-centered evaluation.

</details>


### [167] [HaloGuard 1.0: An Open Weights Constitutional Classifier for Multilingual AI Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02079)
*Navaneeth Sangameswaran,Preetham S,Ashmiya Lenin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: HaloGuard 1.0 是一个基于宪法分类器范式的开源输入安全防护模型，以0.8B参数量在7个提示安全基准上达到平均F1 90.9，性能超越高达27B参数的基线模型，同时将假阳性率控制在4.3，假阴性率控制在9.5。4B变体进一步将F1提升至92.1。该模型采用46条策略和2,940个子类别的自然语言宪法驱动合成数据生成，支持46种语言，并通过持续对抗性红队协议不断强化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源安全防护模型体积庞大，在较小模型下难以同时兼顾高性能和低误报率，且多语言场景下的安全性不足。作者希望构建一个在同等参数量下性能最优、兼具低假阳性和低假阴性率的开源安全防护模型。

Method: 采用宪法分类器范式，以包含46条策略和2,940个子类别的自然语言宪法为核心，驱动合成数据生成。关键技术包括：(1) 一对一配对反事实，固定主题和词汇的同时翻转意图；(2) 双层无害设计，分别针对边界假阳性和基线假阳性；(3) 平衡多语言实现，覆盖46种语言；(4) 持续在线对抗性红队协议。

Result: HaloGuard 1.0-0.8B在7个提示安全基准上平均F1达90.9，假阳性率4.3，假阴性率9.5，优于高达27B参数的基线模型。4B变体平均F1达92.1，假阳性率3.5。对剩余失败的结构化裁定表明，大多数看似漏报的情况为基准误标注而非模型真正遗漏。

Conclusion: HaloGuard 1.0证明，通过精心设计的宪法驱动数据生成策略，小模型也能在安全防护任务上超越大模型。该模型以开源权重发布，为社区提供了高效、低误报的输入安全防护方案。

Abstract: We present HaloGuard 1.0, an open-weights implementation of the constitutional-classifier paradigm for input safety. It achieves state-of-the-art performance on English and multilingual prompt-safety benchmarks at roughly one-tenth the model size of current leading open guard models. The safety constitution is the organising structure of the corpus: a natural-language constitution of 46 policies and 2,940 subcategories drives synthetic data generation, with exhaustive one-to-one paired counterfactuals that hold topic and vocabulary fixed while flipping intent, a two-tier harmless design that separately targets boundary and baseline false positives (FPs), and balanced multilingual materialisation across 46 languages that treats language as a surface form appearing on both sides of the boundary rather than as an adversarial signal. Across seven prompt-safety benchmarks, HaloGuard 1.0-0.8B attains the best average F1 (90.9) of any open guard we evaluate, outperforming baselines up to 27B parameters (over 30 times larger) while holding false-positive rate (FPR) to 4.3 and false-negative rate (FNR) to 9.5. The HaloGuard 1.0-4B variant reaches average F1 of 92.1 and FPR of 3.5, spending its extra capacity on precision rather than recall. A structured adjudication of the remaining failures indicates that most apparent missed-harm cases are benchmark mislabels rather than genuine model misses. An always-on adversarial red-teaming protocol continuously hardens the guard against both content-level and agentic attacks. We release the models as open weights.

### [168] [Unlocking Speech-Text Compositional Powers: Instruction-Following Speech Language Models without Instruction Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02214)
*Congrui Du,Yang Zhang,Kaizhi Qian,Shiyu Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SpeechCombine是一种无需指令微调、仅通过30k小时语音数据预训练和权重组合即可实现语音语言模型指令遵循的方法，避免了传统语音指令微调对大规模数据的需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语音语言模型的指令微调比文本大语言模型更具挑战性，因为它需要同时学习新的模态和广泛的语音特定指令。现有方法复制文本LLM训练范式，但语音序列远长于文本序列，导致难以扩展。

Method: 从文本LLM基座模型出发，在语音话语上进行持续预训练获得语音适配模型，然后直接将此模型权重与文本LLM指令微调版本和基座版本之间的权重差值进行组合。

Result: 这种简单的权重组合策略不仅保留了原始文本LLM的知识和能力，还成功将其迁移到语音领域。

Conclusion: 提出了一种避免依赖大规模语音数据的SLM训练新方向，证明了权重组合可以作为语音指令微调的有效替代方案。

Abstract: Instruction tuning for speech language models (SLMs) is substantially more challenging than for text-based large language models (LLMs), as it requires learning a new modality and a wide range of speech-specific instructions in addition to those supported by text LLMs. Existing SLM training approaches largely replicate the text LLM training paradigm by synthesizing large-scale speech pre-training and instruction-tuning datasets. However, this strategy is difficult to scale, since speech sequences are significantly longer than text sequences. In this paper, we propose SpeechCombine, an instruction-following speech language model trained without any instruction tuning, using only a single round of speech pre-training on 30k hours of data. Starting from a text LLM base model, we perform continuous pre-training on speech utterances to obtain a speech-adapted model, and then directly combine its weights with the weight difference between the instruction-tuned and base versions of the text LLM. Our results show that this simple combination strategy not only preserves the knowledge and capabilities of the original text LLM, but also effectively transfers them to the speech domain. These findings suggest a new direction for SLM training that avoids reliance on massive speech data.

Method: 对ACL Anthology中提及LLM-as-a-Judge的650篇论文进行筛选，聚焦其中33篇关注多语言和低资源设置的论文，进行深度分析，总结评估不一致性、过度信任LLM判断、依赖单一评判模型等问题。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-Judge has become the dominant evaluation paradigm for many natural language generation tasks, due to shortcomings of conventional metrics and high correlations with human judgment, albeit mostly in English. There are now attempts to extend LLM-as-a-Judge to multilingual settings including low-resource languages. However, LLMs have limited proficiency in low-resource languages, and there is often no adequate human validation in these settings. To highlight the scope of the problem and current practices, we explore the use of LLM-as-a-Judge evaluators in ACL Anthology papers focusing on multilingual settings and low-resource languages across a diverse set of tasks. Out of 650 papers mentioning LLM-as-a-judge, only 33 of them focus on low-resource or multilingual settings. Our in-depth analysis of these papers indicates inconsistent evaluation outcomes, a tendency to overtrust LLM judgments in multilingual settings, and the widespread reliance on a single judge model per study. To help the NLP community further, we conclude with recommendations about how to use LLM-as-a-Judge in multilingual and low-resource settings.

Method: CheckRLM从推理链中提取事实性主张以检测和定位知识不一致性，在发现错误后，利用外部知识以最小成本进行精确纠正，确保推理链与正确知识之间的连贯性。

Result: 大量实验表明，CheckRLM显著优于现有基线方法，在长程推理中有效抑制错误累积，同时降低了推理成本。

Abstract: Reasoning Language Models (RLMs) have significantly improved performance on complex tasks by extending the reasoning chain. However, these chains are prone to containing factual errors, particularly in knowledge-intensive tasks. To address this issue, we propose CheckRLM, a framework that improves the reliability of the reasoning process through Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) by timely checking and correcting factual errors. Specifically, CheckRLM extracts factual claims from the reasoning chain to identify and localize subtle knowledge inconsistencies during inference. Upon detection of errors, a refinement mechanism performs minimal-cost yet precise corrections by leveraging external knowledge, ensuring coherence between the reasoning chain and correct knowledge. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CheckRLM substantially outperforms existing baselines, exhibiting a strong capability to mitigate error accumulation in long-horizon reasoning with lower costs. The code and data are available at https://github.com/AI9Stars/CheckRLM.

*Zichao Wei*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 方向性表示将性能瓶颈从符号层转移到神经层，符号层解决了方向性问题，神经层可通过更强的编码器来提升递归深度处理能力，两者互补。

Abstract: Several SLOG test categories explicitly involve directional distinctions (modifier position shifts, argument extraction positions), yet AM-Parser, the previous SOTA, uses an AM algebra whose operations do not encode direction. We redesign the symbolic backend around CCG directed types (deterministic CKY + single linear decoder, 30K learnable parameters). Under the same BERT-base encoder, the system achieves 75.9$\pm$6.4% LF exact match, surpassing AM-Parser (70.8$\pm$4.3%). Per SLOG's own category groupings, gains are highly directional: the CCG system outperforms AM-Parser on all 5 position-shift categories (+29.9pp), while AM-Parser outperforms on all 6 recursive-depth categories. Replacing the encoder with DeBERTa-v3-large yields 90.7$\pm$4.9%, with the largest encoder gains in recursive-depth categories, complementary to directionality's gains. Directional representations shift the bottleneck from the symbolic layer (AM-Parser's 0% category ceiling) to the neural layer, which improves with encoder upgrades.

RUN3 was a RigoChat-based generate-evaluate-regenerate baseline with prompt engineering and LoRA-based adaptation. The official leaderboard reports BLEU-Orig, BLEU-Gold, SARI and BERTScore. During development, additional internal signals were also inspected, including semantic fidelity, readability, lexical simplicity, syntactic clarity and factual consistency. According to official SARI, RUN1 was the best HULAT2 run, with 44.0543 points, followed by RUN2 with 43.1049 and RUN3 with 38.5136. These results indicate that, in this task setting, signal-guided multi-agent routing outperformed the linear regeneration baseline. They also show that adding lexical support did not automatically improve reference-based scores. Further segment-level and document-level analysis are required to assess readability, factual consistency and user-oriented adequacy.

*Benjamin Nichols,Michael Schlichtkrull,Nedjma Ousidhoum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出MEDIAREF，一个公开可用的网络文档知识库，用于支持可复现、低成本的媒体背景检查生成，以解决RAG系统在事实核查中对证据来源可信度评估的依赖性和可复现性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于RAG的自动化事实核查方法通常假设检索到的证据是可靠的，但真实世界的信息可能存在冲突、过时或来自不可靠来源。虽然已有工作通过媒体背景检查(MBC)来评估证据来源的可信度，但生成MBC依赖于昂贵的商业搜索API，限制了可复现性。

Method: 构建MEDIAREF知识库，包含200个媒体来源的网络文档；提出可复现的构建和更新方法；评估主流LLM在MBC生成任务上的表现；通过自动评估和定性评估验证MEDIAREF支持更高质量的MBC生成。

Result: MEDIAREF能够支持可复现、低成本的MBC生成评估，在自动评估和定性评估中均显示出比现有方法更高质量的MBC生成效果。

Conclusion: MEDIAREF通过提供公开可用的知识库，解决了现有媒体背景检查方法依赖付费API的可复现性问题，为RAG系统的源批判推理提供了更可靠、低成本的解决方案。

Abstract: LLM-based retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) is increasingly used for automated fact-checking (AFC) and related tasks. By grounding LLM outputs in retrieved evidence, RAG-based systems provide transparent justifications while allowing external information to be updated independently of the underlying model. However, existing approaches often assume retrieved evidence is reliable, although real-world information may be conflicting, outdated, and can originate from unreliable or biased sources. Recent work on *source-critical reasoning* addresses this challenge through media background checks (MBCs) (Schlichtkrull, 2024), which assess the credibility of evidence sources to support downstream fact verification. However, generating MBCs relies on costly proprietary search APIs, limiting reproducibility. To mitigate this issue, we introduce MEDIAREF, a publicly available knowledge store of web-sourced documents that enables reproducible, low-cost evaluation of MBC generation across 200 media sources. We describe a reproducible methodology for constructing and updating the collection, assess widely used LLMs on the MBC generation task, and demonstrate that MEDIAREF supports higher-quality MBC generation through both automatic and qualitative evaluation.

</details>


### [176] [The Future of NLP may not be at NLP Conferences: Scholarly Migration Patterns in Natural Language Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02416)
*David Jurgens*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: NLP研究正从ACL等核心刊物向机器学习和交叉学科顶会迁移，无论是资深作者还是新晋作者，在LLM时代后的发表重心都发生了显著变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM兴起后，NLP研究的学科重心是否正在从传统核心刊物（如*ACL）向通用机器学习刊物转移。

Method: 基于2010-2026年NLP发表数据，对比LLM时代前后资深作者发表分布变化，分析2019-2024年间新晋作者（以至少3篇一作NLP论文为标准）的发表去向，并运用因果推断技术评估不同刊物类型对引用量的影响。

Result: 资深作者在*ACL主会份额下降19.2pp，在Findings分会上升14.8pp，在通用ML顶会上升8.6pp；新晋作者发表以*ACL为主的占比从84%降至74%，而以通用ML为主的占比从5%升至21%；通用ML顶会具有显著的引用溢价。

Conclusion: NLP研究的发表重心正经历显著迁移，从传统NLP核心刊物向通用机器学习刊物转移。

Abstract: Natural Language Processing (NLP) has traditionally been published in its core disciplinary venues like ACL. However, advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) has led to a blurring of the disciplinary lines between NLP and general Machine Learning (ML), with authors regularly publishing in venues from both fields. Here, we ask whether the disciplinary center of gravity is shifting. Using NLP research published from 2010 to 2026 and studies of both established and new authors, we find that a migration is taking place. First, comparing the pre- and post-LLM eras, established authors lost 19.2pp of share at flagship *ACL main-conference tracks while gaining 14.8pp in the newer Findings tracks, and general ML venues rose 8.6pp, even when adjusting for parallel growth in the fields. Second, among newer authors who debut with at least three first-author NLP-topic papers, the share whose work appears mostly at *ACL venues fell from 84% (2019) to 74% (2024), while the share appearing mostly at general ML venues rose from 5% to 21%. Using causal inference techniques, we estimate that these general ML venues confer a significant citation premium, which influences venue selection. Together, these results point to a significant shift in where NLP research is published.

</details>


### [177] [Language Models as Measurement Apparatus for Culture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02459)
*Kent K. Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文论证NLP文化测量是一种物质-话语实践：测量装置（模型、数据、标注、评估）并非被动记录文化现实，而是参与构成其所测量的文化现实。通过Barad的"施动切割"概念，结合三个影视对话案例研究和三个装置本身的分析，提出一种理论驱动、实证严谨且文化权变的研究范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型越来越多地被用于量化文化现象，但现有研究缺乏对"什么使得这种测量是文化性的"这一根本问题的理论反思。本文旨在揭示NLP文化测量中测量装置与被测现象之间不可分割的纠缠关系。

Method: 采用Barad的"施动切割"(agential cut)概念作为理论框架，通过三个影视对话案例（测量结构、互动和偏差）展示测量中的边界划定，并通过三个装置层面的分析（文化标记的抹除、对历史材料的调谐、施动工作流中的能动性）检视测量装置本身的构成性作用。

Result: 揭示了NLP文化测量的三个关键特征：(1)测量装置的设计选择实质上是现象与仪器之间的边界划定；(2)由于语言模型已内化了大量其所测量的文化材料，这种边界从一开始就是纠缠的；(3)每次施动切割既是一种方法论选择，也是一种伦理承诺。

Conclusion: 提出一种新的研究范式：理论驱动、实证严谨、文化权变，将每次"施动切割"视为自觉的方法论和伦理承诺，从而将文化测量从被动的记录转变为对测量者责任的主动承担。

Abstract: Language models are increasingly used to quantify cultural phenomena, but what makes such measurement distinctively cultural? This paper argues that NLP work on culture is a material-discursive practice: the apparatus -- model, data, annotation, evaluation -- participates in constituting the cultural reality it measures, rather than passively recording it. Drawing on Karen Barad's concept of the agential cut -- the contingent boundary between phenomenon and instrument -- I show that the apparatus's substantive design choices draw such boundaries, and that the boundary is entangled from the start because language models have already internalized much of the cultural material they measure. I illustrate this through three case studies on television and film dialogue (measuring structure, interaction, and deviation) and three examinations of the apparatus itself (erasure of cultural markers, attunement to historical material, and agency in an agentic workflow). This big picture analysis proposes a research program that is theory-driven, empirically rigorous, and culturally contingent, treating each agential cut as a conscious commitment, at once methodological and ethical.

</details>


### [178] [Will Scaling Improve Social Simulation with LLMs?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02464)
*Caleb Ziems,William Held,Su Doga Karaca,David Grusky,Tatsunori Hashimoto,Diyi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过缩放定律研究85个Qwen3架构的Transformer LLM（10^18-10^20 FLOPs预算）及35个更大模型（最高70B参数），发现在意见建模、行为模拟和纵向预测三个社会模拟子领域中，计算规模与模拟保真度之间存在强缩放关系。然而，纵向预测和代表性不足的意见的缩放速度较慢，行为模拟在风险厌恶等认知偏差校准上存在缩放失败，即使从0.5B扩展到8B参数也无显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM社会模拟虽具潜力但保真度不足，研究者希望探究当前语言模型的缩放范式是否能自然解决这一问题，还是模拟保真度与通用能力正交，需要独立的研究关注。

Method: 使用缩放定律方法，在固定计算预算（10^18-10^20 FLOPs）下预训练85个Qwen3架构的Transformer LLM（基于DCLM web文本语料），再评估35个更大开源模型（最高70B参数），研究损失与下游准确率的关系。覆盖三个子领域：意见建模、行为模拟、纵向预测。

Result: 多数意见建模和行为模拟任务随规模快速提升，尤其在英语网络语料代表性好的群体中。纵向预测和代表性不足的意见缩放较慢。行为模拟中，风险厌恶等认知偏差校准和相关性奖励学习等启发式行为存在缩放失败，0.5B到8B参数微调均无显著提升。

Conclusion: 规模提升在多数社会模拟场景中有效，但存在离群任务（尤其低资源领域），改进的可靠性较低，需要额外研究关注。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) social simulations are a promising research method, but they are not yet faithful enough to be adopted widely. In this work, we investigate whether the current scaling paradigm in language modeling is likely to close these gaps, or whether simulation fidelity is orthogonal to general capabilities and therefore deserving of more research attention. We use scaling laws to study the relationship between LLMs' compute scale, general capability benchmarks, and the fidelity of social simulation in three representative sub-domains: opinion modeling, behavioral simulation, and longitudinal forecasting. Surprisingly, we discover strong compute scaling in all three settings, using a suite of 85 transformer LLMs with the Qwen3 architecture pre-trained on the DCLM web text corpus under fixed-compute budgets from $10^{18}$ to $10^{20}$ FLOPs. Then we evaluate 35 larger and more capable open-weight models up to 70B parameters, allowing us to predict downstream accuracy from loss. This reveals that the majority of behavioral and opinion simulation tasks will rapidly improve with scale, particularly when they involve populations that are well-represented in English web corpora. Longitudinal forecasting and underrepresented opinions scale more slowly, especially when they are less correlated with general knowledge and reasoning benchmarks like MMLU. In behavior simulation, scaling fails to improve model calibration with human cognitive biases like risk aversion, as well as human heuristics like learning correlated rewards from related tasks. On these tasks, even fine-tuned models fail to noticeably scale up performance from 0.5B to 8B parameters. Taken together, we conclude that scale will improve social simulations in most settings, but outliers exist, and improvements will be less reliable in low-resource domains.

</details>

Despite limited consumption data, we find that acoustic information alone has a robust association with appeal, even after accounting for title effects. We further validate these findings using more nuanced proprietary engagement metrics. ### [180] [Visually Grounded Self-Reflection for Vision-Language Models via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02490)
*Liyan Tang,Fangcong Yin,Greg Durrett*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出VRRL框架，通过随机掩码轨迹前缀和回放缓冲区经验回滚，增强LVLM在分布偏移下基于视觉的自省能力，显著提升图表理解与空间导航的OOD准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: VRRL包含两个组件：1) 训练时随机掩码轨迹前缀以强调从中期错误恢复而非早期犯错；2) 从经验回放缓冲区引入缓冲回滚，使模型暴露于需要学习修正的多样化失败状态。

Result: 在图表理解与空间导航任务上，VRRL相比标准RL和面向自省的微调基线，显著提升了分布外准确率。

Abstract: Large vision-language models can reason over multimodal inputs by generating textual chains of thought (CoT). A key capability exhibited in CoT reasoning is self-reflection: revisiting earlier decisions and correcting previous errors. However, existing LVLMs often fail to properly attend to visual inputs during reflection, limiting their ability to translate feedback into grounded corrections, especially for out-of-distribution images. To address this issue, we propose a novel reinforcement learning training framework VRRL, with two components explicitly designed to elicit visually grounded self-reflection. First, we randomly mask trajectory prefixes during training to emphasize recovery from incorrect intermediate predictions rather than making early mistakes. Second, we introduce buffered roll-ins from an experience replay buffer to expose the model to diverse failure states that it must learn to correct. We evaluate our approach on visual grounding tasks involving tables and charts, as well as spatial navigation benchmarks. While off-the-shelf and conventionally fine-tuned models degrade substantially under distribution shift, our method substantially improves average out-of-distribution accuracy over standard RL and reflection-oriented fine-tuning baselines by using self-reflection effectively.

</details>

### [182] [LACUNA: A Testbed for Evaluating Localization Precision for LLM Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02513)
*Matteo Boglioni,Thibault Rousset,Siva Reddy,Marius Mosbach,Verna Dankers*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了LACUNA，首个具备参数级定位真实标注的机器遗忘测试平台。通过在OLMo模型中预定义参数注入合成PII，发现现有SOTA遗忘方法虽然输出层面表现良好，但参数级精度极差且易受重浮现攻击。实验表明，精确的参数定位配合简单的梯度遗忘方法即可实现鲁棒擦除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘方法虽然遵循"先定位、后遗忘"的范式，但评估仅在输出层面进行，无法判断是否真正从模型参数中擦除了知识，还是仅掩盖了知识。重浮现攻击的成功更强化了这一担忧，亟需参数级别的评估基准。

Method: 通过掩码持续预训练，将合成个体的PII精确注入到OLMo 1B和7B模型的预定义参数中，创建了具有参数级定位真实标注的测试平台LACUNA；然后利用该平台评估现有SOTA遗忘方法的参数级精度和对重浮现攻击的鲁棒性。

Result: 现有SOTA遗忘方法在输出层面表现良好，但参数级定位精度极差且易受重浮现攻击；当定位精确时，简单的梯度遗忘方法也能实现强擦除效果和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 精确的参数定位是实现鲁棒机器遗忘的关键，LACUNA作为首个参数级评估平台，可补充行为评估并推动基于定位的遗忘方法发展。

Abstract: LLMs memorize sensitive training data, including personally identifiable information (PII), creating a pressing need for reliable post hoc removal methods. Unlearning has emerged as a promising solution, with state-of-the-art(SOTA) methods often following a localize-first, unlearn-second paradigm that targets specific model parameters. However, existing benchmarks evaluate unlearning solely at the output level, leaving open the question of whether unlearning truly erases knowledge from a model's parameters or merely obfuscates it, a concern reinforced by the success of resurfacing attacks. To bridge this gap, we introduce LACUNA: the first unlearning testbed with ground-truth parameter-level localization. LACUNA injects PII of synthetic individuals into predefined parameters of 1B and 7B OLMo-based models via masked continual pretraining, enabling direct evaluation of whether unlearning targets the weights responsible for knowledge storage. We use LACUNA to benchmark current SOTA unlearning methods and find that, despite strong output-level performance, existing methods are highly imprecise and susceptible to resurfacing attacks. We further show that when localization is successful, even a simple gradient-based unlearning method achieves strong erasure and robustness to resurfacing attacks, highlighting the importance of precise unlearning. We release LACUNA to complement behavioral evaluations and drive further advances in robust, localization-based unlearning.

</details>

### [183] [On the structure of constacyclic codes over finite chain rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01771)
*Vaishali Singh,Sucheta Dutt,Ridhima Thakral*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对有限链环上的λ-常循环码，提出了基于最小度数多项式的最小生成元显式构造方法，证明了该构造具有最少的生成元个数，并推导了码的秩与最小度数多项式的关系，最后给出了码为MHDR和MDS的充要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限链环上的常循环码是一类重要的线性码，但此前缺乏任意长度下生成元的显式构造方法和最小生成元数量的理论保证，且对于MHDR和MDS条件的刻画尚不完善。

Method: 利用环 $\mathcal{R}[x]/\langle x^\ell - \lambda\rangle$ 中最小度数多项式进行显式构造；通过分析生成元的性质得到极小生成集；利用剩余域 $\mathbb{F}_q$ 上的扭码刻画MHDR和MDS条件。

Result: (1) 提出了达到最小生成元数量的显式构造；(2) 证明了码的秩 $\ell - n_0$，其中 $n_0$ 为码中最小度数多项式的次数；(3) 给出了码为MHDR和MDS的充要条件，并确定了 $n_0$ 的精确取值使得码为MHDR。

Conclusion: 本文完善了有限链环上任意长度λ-常循环码的结构理论，在最小生成元、秩的计算以及MHDR/MDS码的刻画方面取得了系统性结果。

Abstract: In the present paper, we provide an explicit construction for generators of a $λ$-constacyclic code $\mathcal{C}$ of arbitrary length $\ell$ over a finite chain ring(FCR) $\mathcal{R}$ in terms of certain minimum degree polynomials of the ring $\mathcal{R}[x]/ \langle x^{\ell}-λ\rangle$. Moreover, the proposed construction achieves the minimum possible number of generators. We prove certain properties of this set of generators, using which we obtain a minimal spanning set of $\mathcal{C}$. We also obtain that the rank of $\mathcal{C}$ is $\ell-n_0$, where $n_0$ is the degree of the minimal degree polynomial in $\mathcal{C}$. Finally, we derive necessary and sufficient conditions under which an arbitrary length $λ$-constacyclic code $\mathcal{C}$ over $\mathcal{R}$ is Maximum Hamming Distance with respect to Rank(MHDR) as well as Maximum Distance Separable(MDS) in terms of a torsion code of $\mathcal{C}$ over the residue field $\mathbb{F}_q$ of $\mathcal{R}$. We further determine the exact values for $n_0$ for which $\mathcal{C}$ over $\mathcal{R}$ is MHDR.

</details>


### [184] [Low-Latency Task-Oriented Image Transmission with Opportunistic Spectrum Access](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01921)

TL;DR: 提出一种基于VQ-VAE和机会频谱接入的任务导向传输框架，通过标准数字调制在空闲授权信道上传输离散潜在表示，实现比传统信源信道编码至少79倍和3.3倍的延迟降低，而分类精度仅下降5.7%和2.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统通信系统以可靠数据重建为目标，在频谱有限和衰落信道下依赖分离的信源信道编码，导致高延迟，难以满足低延迟任务导向通信需求。

Method: 采用向量量化变分自编码器（VQ-VAE）学习离散潜在表示，利用机会频谱接入在空闲授权信道上通过标准数字调制传输，并建立包含压缩、块错误、重传和随机信道接入的跨层延迟模型。

Abstract: Communication systems designed for reliable data reconstruction, rather than task-oriented communication, typically rely on separate source and channel coding and incur high latency under limited spectrum availability and fading channels. The AI-powered receiver is still able to reconstruct task-related information from the heavily compressed data. We develop a cross-layer latency model that accounts for compression, block errors, retransmissions, and stochastic channel access. Results on latency-accuracy trade-offs show that the proposed scheme achieves at least 79- and 3.3-fold latency reductions with only 5.7% and 2.4% drops in classification accuracy compared to benchmarks using conventional source and channel coding. The framework enables low-latency communication and reliable task execution even under limited spectrum availability and challenging channel conditions.

### [185] [Generalized Extended Codes with Applications in Entanglement-Assisted Qubit and Qutrit Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02170)
*Yang Li,Martianus Frederic Ezerman,Shitao Li,San Ling,Zhonghua Sun*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 证明广义扩展码与第二类扩展码的Hermitian对偶之间的单项式等价关系；2. 利用向量u相对于C+C^{⊥_H}的位置以及u与C^{⊥_H}最小权码字的关系，刻画广义扩展码的Hermitian hull维数和Hermitian对偶距离；3. 导出同时增大Hermitian hull维数和Hermitian对偶距离的条件；4. 将结果应用于Hermitian构造EAQECCs。

Abstract: We prove that any generalized extended code is monomially equivalent to the Hermitian dual of a code which is closely related to a second kind of extended code of $\C^{\perp_{\rm H}}$. Every $[n+1,k+1]_{q^2}$ linear code $\D$ with $d(\D^{\perp_{\rm H}})>1$ is monomially equivalent to the generalized extended code $\C({\bf u},a)$ of an $[n,k]_{q^2}$ linear code $\C$ for a fixed $a\in\F_{q^2}^{*}$ and some ${\bf u}\in\F_{q^2}^{n}$. We then characterize the Hermitian hull and Hermitian dual distance of $\C({\bf u},a)$ in terms of the position of ${\bf u}$ relative to $\C+\C^{\perp_{\rm H}}$ and the interaction between ${\bf u}$ and the minimum weight codewords of $\C^{\perp_{\rm H}}$, respectively. We obtain explicit criteria to independently control the expected Hermitian hull dimension and Hermitian dual distance of $\C({\bf u},a)$. In particular, several conditions for simultaneously increasing the Hermitian hull dimension and the Hermitian dual distance of $\C({\bf u},a)$ are derived. Applying these results to the Hermitian construction for EAQECCs gives us $267$ new EA qubit codes of lengths $n \leq 40$ and $14$ new EA qutrit codes of lengths $n \leq 25$ compared to the best-known codes in Grassl's code tables and the imporvements recorded in very recent works in the literature. Among the new parameter sets, we confirm improvements for $236$ qubit and $8$ qutrit codes.

### [186] [The Weight Distribution of the Third-Order Reed-Muller Code of Length 2048](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02365)
*Kirill Khoruzhii,Patrick Gelß,Sebastian Pokutta*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文计算了长度2048的三阶Reed-Muller码RM(3,11)的权重分布，通过评估所有3691560个非零GL(10,2)-轨道上f+RM(2,10)的陪集权重枚举器完成。关键结构定理：非退化布尔三次形式允许非退化超平面限制，除每个奇数维中的单个轨道外。同时确定了每个三次形式的二阶非线性度：RM(2,10)在RM(3,10)中的相对覆盖半径为408，覆盖半径下界从400提高到408；RM(6,10)在RM(7,10)中的相对覆盖半径上界改进为32。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Reed-Muller码的权重分布和覆盖半径是编码理论中的基本问题，计算高阶RM码的精确权重分布具有重大挑战性。RM(3,11)的权重分布此前未知，而RM(2,10)的覆盖半径下界长期停留在400，需要改进。

Method: 利用结构定理（非退化三次形式存在非退化超平面限制，除奇数维中一个轨道外），将RM(3,11)权重分布问题约化为评估所有3691560个非零GL(10,2)-轨道上f+RM(2,10)的陪集权重枚举器。结合互补启发式搜索改进覆盖半径上界。

Result: 确定了RM(3,11)的完整权重分布；RM(2,10)在RM(3,10)中的相对覆盖半径为408（由179个轨道达到），将覆盖半径下界从400提升至408；RM(6,10)在RM(7,10)中的相对覆盖半径上界从50改进至32。

Conclusion: 完成了RM(3,11)权重分布的精确计算，显著改进了Reed-Muller码覆盖半径的已知下界和上界，展示了结构定理在简化高阶RM码分析中的有效性。

Abstract: We compute the weight distribution of the third-order Reed--Muller code RM(3,11) of length 2048. The weight enumerator is assembled from the coset weight enumerators of f+RM(2,10), evaluated for representatives of all 3691560 nonzero GL(10,2)-orbits of Boolean cubic forms in ten variables. The computation rests on a structural theorem: a nondegenerate Boolean cubic form admits a nondegenerate hyperplane restriction, except for a single orbit in each odd dimension. The same pass determines the second-order nonlinearity of every cubic form: the relative covering radius of RM(2,10) in RM(3,10) is 408, attained on 179 orbits. This raises the best known lower bound on the covering radius of RM(2,10) from 400 to 408. A complementary heuristic search shows that the relative covering radius of RM(6,10) in RM(7,10) is at most 32, improving the previous bound of 50.

### [187] [Generalized Rank Weight and Extended Generalized Poset Weight Defined For Codes Over Rings: A Galois Connection Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02377)
*Yang Xu,Haibin Kan,Guangyue Han*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文通过伽罗瓦连接方法，系统研究了环上码的广义秩权重（GRWs）和扩展广义偏序集权重（EGPWs），将多种编码性质（如窃听信道安全、Singleton界、MDS/MRD码刻画等）统一为伽罗瓦连接框架，并在主理想环（特别是链环）上建立了GRWs的Singleton界与Wei型对偶定理，在拟Frobenius环上统一了EGPWs的Wei型对偶定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于环上码的广义权重理论较为分散，缺乏统一的数学框架；同时，伽罗瓦连接方法在编码理论中的应用尚未被系统探索。本文旨在利用伽罗瓦连接统一刻画广义权重相关的多种编码性质，并将结果推广到更一般的环上。

Method: 采用伽罗瓦连接（Galois connection）作为核心数学工具，首先将窃听信道安全下降、Gabidulin码与Delsarte码的广义权重关系、Singleton界、MDS/MRD/i-MDS/i-MRD/evasive子空间等性质重新表述为伽罗瓦连接形式。然后，将GRWs和秩分布（rank profiles）推广到主理想环（尤其是链环）上的模，建立相应的Singleton界和Wei型对偶定理。最后，提出EGPWs和扩展偏序集分布（extended poset profiles），将其推广到具有合成列的模上，并在任意拟Frobenius环上统一了已有的两个Wei型对偶定理。

Result: 1) 多种编码性质（安全下降、广义权重关系、Singleton界、MDS/MRD等码的刻画、evasive性质）均可统一用伽罗瓦连接重新表述。2) 在链环上的模中，建立了GRWs的Singleton界和Wei型对偶定理，刻画了MRD、近MRD、对偶拟MRD码，并确定了它们的GRWs；还刻画了i-MRD码，建立了链环上(h,h)-evasive码的scattered界。3) 提出了EGPWs和扩展偏序集分布，在任意拟Frobenius环上统一了[32]和[33]中的两个Wei型对偶定理。

Conclusion: 伽罗瓦连接是一个强有力的统一框架，可以将编码理论中多种广义权重相关性质进行系统化表述和推广。本文不仅将GRWs和EGPWs推广到更一般的环上，还统一了已有的对偶定理，为后续在更广泛环类上研究码的权重结构提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we study generalized rank weights (GRWs) and extended generalized poset weight (EGPWs) of codes over rings via a Galois connection approach. First, we show that various coding-theoretic properties related to generalized weights, including security drops of a code employed in wire-tap channel of type II, connections between generalized weights of a Gabidulin code and its associated Delsarte code, (generalized) Singleton bound, MDS discrepancy of a code, characterizations of MDS, near MDS, $i$-MDS, MRD, near MRD, $i$-MRD, (dually) quasi-MRD codes as well as evasive property of subspaces, can be reformulated in terms of Galois connections. Next, we study GRWs and rank profiles defined for modules over principal ideal rings, especially those over chain rings. Generalizing GRWs defined for vector spaces over fields, we establish a singleton bound and a Wei-type duality theorem, characterize MRD, near MRD and dually quasi-MRD codes and determine their GRWs; moreover, we characterize $i$-MRD codes and establish a scattered bound for $(h,h)$-evasive codes over chain rings, generalizing counterpart result established for vector space over finite fields. Finally, we propose and study EGPWs and extended poset profiles defined for modules with a composition series, which in fact form a Galois connection. Generalizing EGPWs defined for modules over finite Galois rings, we establish a Wei-type duality theorem for modules over arbitrary quasi-Frobenius rings, which unifies the two Wei-type duality theorems derived in both \cite{32} and \cite{33}.

### [188] [Ultra-Low-Cost Hybrid Beamforming: A New Static-Connection Architecture with Sparse Phase-Shifter Sharing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02393)
*Honghao Wang,Qingqing Wu,Yifei Wu,Yuxuan Chen,Wen Chen,Derrick Wing Kwan Ng*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种静态连接稀疏移相器架构用于超低成本子连接混合波束赋形，通过优化移相器与天线的固定连接矩阵，在单RF链和多RF链场景下分别减少37.5%和62.5%的移相器数量，同时保持大部分波束赋形性能，避免深度零陷和栅瓣退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统子连接混合波束赋形架构中每个天线仍需专用移相器，导致布局面积、布线、校准和控制开销巨大。为降低硬件成本与复杂度，亟需探索移相器共享的静态连接方案。

Method: 提出稀疏移相器静态连接架构，子阵列内天线通过优化固定连接矩阵共享移相器。单RF链场景转化为天线分组问题并给出结构性质与高效算法；多RF链场景提出QoS-MM算法处理混合离散-连续优化。

Conclusion: 实现硬件高效混合波束赋形的关键在于通过优化移相器连接拓扑保留模拟域自由度，而非单纯减少移相器数量。

Abstract: Hybrid beamforming is a promising solution for high-frequency multi-antenna wireless systems, but its implementation is constrained by the cost and complexity of analog phase-shifter (PS) networks. Although sub-connected architectures simplify the analog network, their conventional realization still requires a dedicated PS for each antenna, causing considerable layout area, wiring, calibration, and control overheads. To address this issue, this paper proposes a novel static-connection architecture with sparse PSs for ultra-low-cost sub-connected hybrid beamforming, where antennas within each sub-array share a PS through an optimized fixed PS-to-antenna connection matrix. The proposed architecture preserves static connections while enabling dynamic beam control via adaptive PS phase-shift adjustments and digital precoding. For the single-radio-frequency (RF)-chain scenario, the sparse-PS connection design is transformed into an antenna-grouping problem, with analytically characterized structural properties and an efficient algorithm. For the multi-RF-chain scenario, we develop a quality-of-service (QoS)-majorization-minimization (MM) algorithm to handle the mixed discrete-continuous optimization problem. Numerical results demonstrate that the proposed architecture reduces the PS count while preserving most beamforming capability of the traditional full-PS sub-connected architecture. In particular, the proposed design achieves PS-count reductions of 37.5% and 62.5% in single-RF-chain and multi-RF-chain systems, respectively, while avoiding deep-null and grating-lobe degradations associated with deterministic connection schemes. These results provide engineering insights into static sparse-PS sharing: the key to hardware-efficient hybrid beamforming is not merely reducing the PS count, but also preserving essential analog-domain degrees of freedom through optimized PS connection topologies.

### [189] [TO-Master: an LLM-agent framework for automated topology optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01812)
*Haoju Lin,Wenchang Zhang,Weipeng Xu,Xiang Li,Tian Xu,Tianju Xue*

TL;DR: 本文提出TO-Master，一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体框架，通过自然语言对话式交互和工具编排，自动化完成有限元拓扑优化的几何准备、网格生成、边界条件设置、求解和后处理等流程，无需用户编写代码即可复现基准算例并求解复杂工程问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Topology optimization (TO) has become a mature computational design method, but using it still requires substantial manual effort in geometry preparation, mesh generation, boundary-condition assignment, solver setup, and postprocessing. This implementation barrier limits the use of TO outside expert workflows, even when differentiable finite element solvers are available. This work introduces TO-Master, a large language model (LLM) agent framework that turns finite-element-based TO into a conversational, tool-orchestrated workflow. From natural language instructions and optional mesh, geometry, or image inputs, the agent selects computational tools, constructs finite element TO models, checks meshes and boundary conditions, and launches sensitivity-based optimization with typed solver arguments. The framework supports generated and uploaded meshes, image-to-mesh conversion, 2D and 3D structural compliance minimization, thermal conduction, multiple load cases, stress-constrained optimization, and engineering geometries. Numerical experiments show that TO-Master can reproduce standard benchmark results and solve more complex engineering examples while returning optimized results, field distributions, convergence histories, and interactive artifacts without user-written code. An instruction ablation study further shows that tool-usage rules, internal reasoning guidance, and few-shot examples are critical for robust formulation under ambiguous user input. By combining LLM-agent orchestration with deterministic finite element and optimization tools, TO-Master removes the burden of trivial setup and routine model construction, lowers the modeling barrier of TO, and preserves a reliable numerical workflow. The TO-Master platform is available online at https://www.bohrium.com/en/apps/to-master.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两阶段分布式机制设计：第一阶段每个组基于本地代理报告独立选择一对候选位置作为代表；第二阶段从所有组的代表集中选择最终的两个设施位置。聚焦于确定性策略proof分布式机制类，分析其在四种社会目标下的失真界。

Abstract: This paper investigates a constrained distributed heterogeneous two-facility location problem under the max-variant cost model. In this setting, a set of agents with private locations on the real line is partitioned into disjoint groups. The constraint stipulates that facilities must be situated within a given multiset of candidate locations, with the restriction that each candidate location can host at most one facility. Under the max-variant model, an agent's individual cost is defined as the distance from their location to the farthest facility. Our objective is to design strategyproof distributed mechanisms that incentivize agents to report their locations truthfully while approximating social objectives. Such mechanisms operate in two stages: first, for each group, a pair of candidate locations is selected as representatives based solely on local reports; subsequently, the mechanism outputs two final facility locations from the set of all representatives. We focus on a class of deterministic strategyproof distributed mechanisms and establish constant lower and upper bounds on the distortion under four social objectives: Average-of-Average, Max-of-Max, Average-of-Max, and Max-of-Average costs.

### [191] [Facility Location Game with Envy Ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02330)
*Yuan Ding,Wenjing Liu,Xin Chen,Qizhi Fang,Qingqin Nong*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究实数线上单设施选址博弈问题，以"嫉妒比率"（公平分配中的平等主义指标）作为优化目标，该指标定义为任意两个代理效用比值的最大值。作者关注能够最小化嫉妒比率的策略proof或群体策略proof机制，并在两种自然场景下展开研究：设施和所有代理位置均限制在固定区间内；代理位置可在实数线上任意点但设施限制在相对区间内。两种场景下均获得了最优解和最优确定性策略proof机制（同时也是群体策略proof的）。在第一种场景下给出了随机策略proof机制的下界；在第二种场景下给出了随机策略proof机制的下界及两个上界。

Method: 采用机制设计方法，分别在两种约束场景（设施-代理同区间限制；代理无限制-设施相对区间限制）下，分析确定性及随机策略proof机制的最优性能，给出下界与上界。

Result: 两种场景下均得到了最优解和最优确定性策略proof（且群体策略proof）机制；第一种场景下给出了随机策略proof机制的下界；第二种场景下给出了随机策略proof机制的下界及两个上界。

Conclusion: 成功将嫉妒比率引入设施选址博弈，在策略proof约束下为不同场景提供了最优机制设计与理论界限，拓展了公平设施选址的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the one-facility location game on a real line with a new objective called envy ratio. The envy ratio, which is adopted from fair division and represents the egalitarianism, is defined as the maximum over the ratios between any two agents' utilities. We are interested in strategyproof or group strategyproof mechanisms that can minimize the envy ratio objective.
  We consider the model in two settings that can capture natural scenarios: the facility location and all the agents' locations are restricted on a fixed interval; every agent's location can be any point on the real line but the facility location is restricted on a relative interval. In both settings, we obtain the optimal solution and the best deterministic strategyproof mechanism which is also group strategyproof. In the first setting, we provide a lower bound for randomized strategyproof mechanisms. In the second setting, we give a lower bound and two upper bounds for randomized strategyproof mechanisms.

</details>

### [192] [PACE: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Plausible and Actionable Counterfactual Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01306)
*Pavel Iakovets,Liyanapathiranage Sudeepika Wajirakumari Samarathunga,Martin Thomas Horsch,Fadi Al Machot*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PACE，一种模块化神经符号框架，将神经预测模型与符号推理（ASP规则）相结合，在生成反事实解释时显式融入领域知识和干预约束，确保解释的可行性与可操作性。在Adult Income数据集上的案例研究展示了符号约束在平衡反事实有效性与可行性方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反事实解释方法虽能生成改变预测结果的输入变化，但缺乏显式机制来融入领域知识和干预约束，导致推荐往往不现实或不可行。

Method: PACE框架采用模块化神经符号架构，分离预测与推理：神经预测模型（如MLP）负责分类，符号推理层（ASP规则）在反事实生成过程中强制执行领域特定约束，显式建模可行干预。

Result: 在Adult Income数据集上，结合MLP分类器与ASP规则（编码对教育、职业、工作时间的可行修改，同时保留不可变属性），结果表明符号约束生成的反事实解释更好地满足领域特定的可行性要求，揭示了反事实有效性与合理性之间的权衡。

Conclusion: PACE展示了神经符号方法在生成透明、可行性感知的反事实解释方面的潜力，具有模型无关性，适用于需要现实决策支持的领域。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations explain machine learning predictions by identifying minimal input changes that would alter a model's decision. Although many existing methods successfully generate prediction-changing alternatives, they often produce unrealistic or infeasible recommendations due to a lack of explicit mechanisms for incorporating domain knowledge and intervention constraints. Neuro-symbolic AI offers a promising direction by combining data-driven predictive models with symbolic reasoning capable of representing human-understandable rules and feasible actions. This paper presents PACE, a modular neuro-symbolic framework for generating feasibility-aware counterfactual explanations. The framework separates prediction and reasoning into two components: a neural predictive model for classification and a symbolic reasoning layer that enforces domain-specific constraints during counterfactual generation. By explicitly modeling feasible interventions, the framework produces explanations consistent with domain knowledge while remaining interpretable and actionable. The approach is model-agnostic and adaptable to domains requiring realistic decision support. A case study is conducted on the Adult Income dataset, combining a multilayer perceptron classifier with Answer Set Programming (ASP) rules encoding feasible modifications to education, occupation, and working hours while preserving immutable attributes. Results highlight the trade-off between counterfactual validity and plausibility and show that symbolic constraints yield explanations that better satisfy domain-specific feasibility requirements, illustrating the potential of neuro-symbolic methods for transparent, feasibility-aware counterfactual explanation in explainable AI.

</details>


### [193] [Auto-FL-Research: Agentic Search for Federated Learning Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01366)
*Holger R. Roth,Ziyue Xu,Chester Chen,Daguang Xu,Peter Cnudde,Andrew Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了Auto-FL-Research (AFR)，一个用于联邦学习算法配方搜索的约束编码智能体工作流，在多个联邦学习任务上进行了评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习研究中的算法选择（优化器、聚合规则、训练调度等）繁多且相互影响，人工探索成本高，公平比较困难。

Method: 设计约束编码智能体工作流AFR，智能体可提出并实现候选训练算法（服务器聚合规则、客户端更新调度、局部目标、模型变体），任务配置固定变异面、计算预算、通信约束和评估方式，记录候选分数、运行时、编辑文件等。

Result: 在5个FLamby医疗任务和6个LEAF任务上评估，5次种子重复实验在4个FLamby任务和5个LEAF任务上获得增益，但也暴露出种子敏感性和搜索选择的失败案例。

Conclusion: 智能体生成的候选可区分为：重复的FL机制、固定表面调优效应和选中的单次运行伪影；部分增益来自FL配方变更，部分可通过固定表面标量控制恢复，或在重复/保留评估下失效。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) research often depends on many small but consequential algorithmic choices: optimizer variants, server aggregation rules, local training schedules, normalization, regularization, and model architecture. These choices are expensive to explore manually and difficult to compare fairly when candidate changes can also alter the FL training or evaluation path. In this work, we present Auto-FL-Research (AFR), a constrained coding-agent workflow for FL algorithmic recipe search. Agents may propose and implement candidate training algorithms, including server aggregation rules, client update schedules, local objectives, and registered model variants, while task profiles fix the mutation surface, compute budget, communication contract, and final model evaluation. Each campaign records candidate scores, runtime, edited files, artifacts, and failure status. We evaluate AFR on five healthcare cross-silo FLamby tasks and on grouped-client profiles for the five fixed LEAF datasets plus the LEAF synthetic task. Five-seed repeat evaluations support gains on four FLamby tasks and five of six LEAF profiles, while also exposing seed-sensitive and search-selected failure cases. Same-budget controls show that several gains correspond to FL-recipe changes, whereas other improvements are recovered by fixed-surface scalar controls or fail under repeat or held-out evaluation. These mixed outcomes are part of the contribution: they show how agent-generated candidates can be separated into repeated FL mechanisms, fixed-surface tuning effects, and selected single-run artifacts.

</details>


### [194] [The Wiola Architecture for Efficient Small Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01394)
*Aryuemaan Kumar Chowdhury,Afreen Shaik,Yaparla Bhargavi,Brahma Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Wiola 是一个完全原创的小型语言模型架构，包含五种全新组件：螺旋旋转位置编码（SRPE）、门控跨层注意力（GCLA）、自适应Token合并（ATM）、双流前馈网络（DSFF）和WiolaRMSNorm，提供四种规模（120M-1.5B参数）并兼容HuggingFace生态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SLM架构（如GPT、LLaMA等）在结构上存在同质化问题，论文旨在从第一性原理出发设计一种完全原创的架构，探索替代现有主流模型家族的新范式。

Method: 提出五种独立创新组件：SRPE（3D螺旋流形位置编码）、GCLA（跨层软注意力访问前两层压缩摘要）、ATM（动态合并语义冗余相邻Token）、DSFF（双并行流前馈网络+可学习门控）、WiolaRMSNorm（引入逐维可学习偏移向量防止表示坍缩）。

Result: 发布四种规模（120M/360M/700M/1.5B参数）的Wiola模型，提供完整数学推导、复杂度分析和系统对比（vs GPT-2/LLaMA-2/Mistral），全部22个架构单元测试通过，兼容HuggingFace Transformers。

Conclusion: Wiola证明了从零设计原创SLM架构的可行性，为语言模型架构创新提供了新的方向，且具备实际可用性和生态兼容性。

Abstract: We present Wiola, a fully original Small Language Model (SLM) architecture built from first principles, sharing no structural lineage with any existing model family including GPT, LLaMA, Mistral, or Falcon. Wiola introduces five independently novel components: (i) Spiral Rotary Positional Encoding (SRPE), which embeds token positions on a three-dimensional helical manifold combining absolute, relative, and hierarchical positional signals; (ii) Gated Cross-Layer Attention (GCLA), providing each decoder layer with soft cross-attention access to compressed summaries of two preceding layers for inter-layer coherence; (iii) Adaptive Token Merging (ATM), which dynamically merges se mantically redundant adjacent tokens in middle network layers to reduce attention complexity without information loss; (iv) Dual Stream Feed-Forward (DSFF), replacing the conventional MLP with two parallel streams fused by a learned per-dimension gate; and (v) WiolaRMSNorm, a modified normalisation introducing a per-dimension learned offset vector that prevents representation collapse. We provide complete mathematical derivations, architectural block diagrams, complexity analyses, and systematic comparisons against GPT-2, LLaMA-2, and Mistral. Wiola is released in four sizes (120M, 360M, 700M, and 1.5B parameters) and is fully compatible with the HuggingFace Transformers ecosystem, with all 22 architectural unit tests passing.

</details>


### [195] [Agent4cs: A Multi-agent System for Code Summarization in Large Hierarchical Codebases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01425)
*Yongjian Tang,Ezgi Sarikayak,Doruk Tuncel,Jie M. Zhang,Thomas Runkler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一个名为Agent4cs的多智能体框架，采用自底向上方式对大型代码库进行摘要生成，包含摘要生成、关键词提取和质量保证三个智能体，在7个前沿模型上评估，语义一致性平均提升8%，关键词覆盖率最高提升38%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码摘要方案多依赖单一语言模型，将源代码视为平面文本进行处理，未能充分利用代码库中丰富的层次依赖和结构化信息，且难以应对混淆结构和不完整文档的大型复杂代码库。

Method: 提出多智能体框架Agent4cs，采用自底向上的摘要生成方式：摘要生成智能体负责生成稳健摘要；关键词提取智能体主动识别子文件夹中的关键信息；质量保证智能体迭代优化输出的可读性、连贯性和完整性。

Result: 在7个前沿模型上评估，相比两种结构化提示基线方法，各文件夹级别的语义一致性平均提升8%；在真实数据集上，归一化关键词覆盖率的提升高达38%。

Conclusion: Agent4cs通过多智能体协作和自底向上的层次化处理方式，有效提升了大型代码库摘要的质量，验证了利用代码库层次结构和多智能体协作优于单一模型平面文本处理方法。

Abstract: Understanding large, complex codebases, especially those with obfuscated structures and incomplete documentation, remains a significant challenge. Existing code summarization solutions often rely on a single language model or coding assistant like Claude Code, and treat source code as flat text, underutilizing the rich interdependencies and hierarchical information within a repository. To address these shortcomings, we propose Agent4cs - a multi-agent framework that summarizes large codebases in a bottom-up fashion, where a summarization agent focuses on producing robust summaries; a keyword-extraction agent proactively identifies critical information from subfolders; and a quality-assurance agent iteratively refines the outputs for readability, coherence, and completeness. Evaluated on 7 frontier models, Agent4cs improves semantic consistency across all folder levels by average 8% compared to two structured prompting baselines with code segments. Furthermore, extensive evaluation on real-world datasets demonstrates up to 38% gains in normalized keyword coverage rate over the same baselines.

</details>


### [196] [When Should Service Agents Reconsider? Difficulty-Routed Control in Customer-Service Operations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01426)
*Qian Chen,Chengyuan Liu,Xin Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种"难度路由服务控制架构"，根据操作耦合度将对话分流至常规路径或升级路径，升级路径采用冲突感知通信和写前重审机制，在零售和航空任务中提升了有操作冲突的服务请求的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主客服智能体从对话交互转向操作执行（退款、改单、预订变更等），需要解决服务控制问题：既要保持常规服务快速低摩擦，又要防止因客户指令、策略约束、记录与后端写入交互而引发的操作错误。

Method: 提出难度路由服务控制架构：轻量路由器将常规会话保留在低成本基线路径，将操作耦合度高的会话路由至升级工作流。升级路径使用冲突感知通信和写前重审机制，在关键后端写入前集中推理和安全检查，而非对所有会话统一施加额外控制。

Result: 在τ²-bench零售任务中，该方法在有操作冲突的服务请求上持续提升可靠性；路由证据表明更强控制定向于冲突请求而非泛化到常规会话。对话和工具调用剖析显示增益来自证据收集、写入分离和写前重审，而非无差别扩展交互。案例分析显示升级工作流保留了备用方案、将记录绑定到正确动作、序列化写入并分解多实体请求。航空任务验证了相同逻辑在预订操作中的推广性。

Conclusion: 难度路由架构能有效区分常规与高风险操作会话，将推理和防护集中在真正需要审慎处理的后端写入前环节，为自主客服智能体的安全执行提供了可扩展的方案。

Abstract: Autonomous customer-service agents are shifting from conversational interfaces toward operational execution roles: they retrieve firm records, apply service policies, and execute backend writes such as refunds, cancellations, exchanges, order modifications, and reservation changes. This shift creates a service-control problem: firms must keep routine service fast and low-friction while preventing operational errors on requests where customer instructions, policy constraints, firm records, and backend writes interact. We propose a difficulty-routed service-control architecture that asks when service agents should reconsider before acting. A lightweight router keeps routine sessions on a low-cost baseline path and routes operationally coupled sessions to an escalated workflow. The escalated path uses conflict-aware communication and write-triggered reconsideration to concentrate deliberation and safeguards before consequential backend writes, rather than applying additional control uniformly across all service sessions. We evaluate the architecture on human-verified retail and airline tasks from $τ^{2}$-bench. In retail, the method improves reliability consistently on service requests with operational conflict. Routing evidence shows that stronger control is directed toward conflicted requests rather than broadly applied to routine ones. Dialogue and tool-use profiles suggest that gains do not come from indiscriminate interaction expansion or broader tool chains; instead, added turns and tool calls support evidence gathering, write separation, and pre-write reconsideration. Case-level evidence shows that the escalated workflow preserves fallback plans, binds retrieved records to the correct action, sequences writes, and decomposes multi-entity requests. Airline results extend the same service-control logic to reservation operations.

</details>


### [197] [CreativityNeuro: Steering Language Model Weights to Improve Divergent Thinking and Reduce Mode Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01433)
*Samuel Schapiro,Core Francisco Park,Felix Sosa,Lav R. Varshney*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出CreativityNeuro，一种无需数据、无需重训练的无梯度方法，通过对比权重引导增强LLM的 divergent thinking（发散思维），在多项创造力测试上显著提升表现，并有效减少模式坍缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在开放性问题中倾向于生成相似回答（人工蜂群效应），缺乏发散性思维，现有方法依赖行为数据或梯度微调，亟需轻量级、可泛化的解决方案。

Method: 采用对比权重引导（contrastive weight steering），在不依赖数据、重训练或梯度微调的情况下，直接调整模型权重以增强发散性思维。

Result: 在DAT任务上提升高达14个人类百分位点；在大规模人类评估（N=720）的AUT和Task Task中，在原创性、惊喜度和创造力上有显著提升；在所有三项任务中均减少模式坍缩；权重引导相比激活引导具有更好的跨任务泛化能力。

Conclusion: CreativityNeuro能有效提升LLM的发散思维并减少模式坍缩，且无需数据、重训练或梯度微调，是一种简洁有效的增强LLM创造力的方法。

Abstract: Divergent thinking is a crucial aspect of creativity, yet large language models (LLMs) tend to consistently generate similar responses to open-ended questions, in what has been termed the artificial hivemind effect. Here, we introduce CreativityNeuro, a data-free method for enhancing divergent thinking in LLMs via contrastive weight steering. We evaluate our method across multiple creativity assessments and report several main findings. On the Divergent Association Task (DAT), a vocabulary-space creativity test, CreativityNeuro improves performance by up to 14 human percentile points. Next, in a large-scale human evaluation (N=720) on the Alternative Uses Test (AUT) and the Task Task, CreativityNeuro achieves significant improvements in originality, surprise, and creativity, transferring to longer-form and more open-ended tasks. Importantly, we find that across all three tasks, CreativityNeuro demonstrably reduces measures of mode collapse. Moreover, activation steering achieves comparable performance to CreativityNeuro on the DAT, but it does not transfer to the AUT and Task Task, demonstrating the effectiveness of weight-space steering in generalizing to unseen tasks. In conclusion, CreativityNeuro improves divergent thinking and reduces mode collapse without requiring behavioral data, re-training, or gradient-based fine-tuning, providing a straightforward way to enhance LLM performance in creative domains.

</details>


### [198] [Discrete Diffusion Language Models for Interactive Radiology Report Drafting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01436)
*Max Van Puyvelde,Halil Ibrahim Gulluk,Wim Van Criekinge,Olivier Gevaert*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文验证了扩散语言模型（DiffusionGemma-26B）在医学视觉问答任务上与同规模自回归模型（Gemma-4-26B）性能持平或更优，解码速度提升3.5-4.4倍，并展现了自回归模型缺乏的任意顺序填充能力，更适合真实临床报告场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学基础模型目前几乎全部采用自回归架构，而扩散语言模型在文本生成领域已展现竞争力，但在医学场景下尚未被充分探索。作者旨在验证扩散模型能否替代自回归模型用于医学视觉问答，并利用其双向去噪特性解决临床报告的实际需求。

Method: 将混合专家扩散语言模型DiffusionGemma-26B与其同规模自回归模型Gemma-4-26B在医学视觉问答数据集上采用相同LoRA微调方案进行对比，使用对冗长性鲁棒的LLM裁判评分，并评估解码速度和任意顺序填充能力。

Result: 扩散模型在所有医学视觉问答数据集上与自回归模型性能持平或更优，微调后的模型（3.8B活跃参数）可与前沿视觉语言模型竞争，解码速度提升3.5-4.4倍，并具备自回归模型无法实现的任意顺序填充能力。

Conclusion: 扩散语言模型在医学视觉问答任务中不仅能达到自回归模型的性能，还因解码速度和任意顺序填充能力的优势，更适合处理临床报告文本中因临床医生和机构差异导致的碎片化与不一致性问题。

Abstract: Diffusion language models, which generate text by denoising a token canvas bidirectionally instead of emitting tokens left to right, have become competitive with autoregressive (AR) generation. Medical foundation models, however, remain almost entirely autoregressive. We adapt a mixture-of-experts diffusion language model, DiffusionGemma-26B, and benchmark it against its same-size AR sibling Gemma-4-26B under an identical LoRA recipe on medical visual question answering datasets, scored by a verbosity-robust LLM judge. Diffusion matches or exceeds AR on all of them, and the finetuned model (3.8B active) is competitive with frontier vision-language models; its decoding is also 3.5-4.4x faster. Beyond this parity, the diffusion model offers a drafting capability AR lacks: any-order infill. Because the canvas is denoised bidirectionally, a radiologist can fix report fragments and have the model fill the text between them, an operation inherent to diffusion but not to autoregression, which is subpar at it. This suits real reports, which are often terse or inconsistent across clinicians and institutions.

</details>


### [199] [Beyond Next-Token Prediction: An RLVR Proof of Concept for Tool-Use Agents on Atlassian Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01465)
*Karthikeya Aditya Vissa,Sankalp Mane,Ananya Mantravadi,Harshit Rajgarhia,Abhishek Mukherji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出使用基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）直接在目标环境中训练小模型，以解决大语言模型在SaaS API调用中因预测下一个token与具体执行不匹配导致的无声失败问题。在五个高保真合成环境（Jira REST v3和Confluence v2）上的实验表明，GRPO训练的Qwen3.5-4B在非退化场景中将平均奖励从0.35–0.92提升至0.95–1.00，最大提升为Confluence页面创建（0.35→1.00）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型训练目标是预测下一个token，而非在特定API中执行动作。在B端SaaS工作流中，这种目标不匹配导致静默失败：遗漏必填字段、幻觉工具、单次读取后提前终止。现有方法缺乏针对小众企业级API的端到端优化方案。

Method: 构建五个模拟Jira REST v3和Confluence v2 API架构的合成环境，奖励完全从工具调用轨迹计算（无需真实API、学习型裁判或人工标注）。使用GRPO算法对Qwen3-1.7B和Qwen3.5-4B进行训练，验证奖励与训练检查器一致。

Result: 在四个非退化奖励场景中，RL训练策略将平均奖励从4B基线的0.35–0.92提升至0.95–1.00。Confluence页面创建提升最大（0.35→1.00）。第五个场景（ticket-transition）奖励饱和，4B基线已达到最优。

Conclusion: RLVR可有效优化小模型在特定企业API上的执行性能，但存在两个主要局限：手工构建可验证奖励无法扩展到更多端点；奖励函数设计需避免饱和问题。

Abstract: Large language models are trained to predict the next token, not to act inside a specific API. In niche enterprise SaaS workflows -- where success means hitting the right endpoint with the right nested arguments in the right order -- this objective mismatch shows up as silent failures: dropped required fields, hallucinated tools, or early stops after a single read. We ask whether Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), applied directly in the target environment, closes the gap. As a proof of concept we build a suite of five synthetic environments emulating the Jira REST v3 and Confluence v2 APIs at schema fidelity; rewards are computed entirely from the tool-call trace, with no live API, no learned judge, and no human label in the loop. Scoring prompted Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen3.5-4B on the same checkers that drive GRPO training, we find that on the four scenarios whose rewards are non-degenerate the RL-trained policy lifts average reward from a 4B-baseline range of 0.35--0.92 to 0.95--1.00, with the largest single gain on Confluence page creation ($0.35 \rightarrow 1.00$). We position this as a preliminary step toward outcome-optimised small models for niche enterprise APIs, and foreground two limitations a workshop reader should weigh: hand-crafting verifiable rewards does not scale beyond the handful of endpoints reported here, and one of our five scenarios (ticket-transition) has a saturating reward shape that the prompted 4B already maxes out.

</details>

Result: 纯RL达到18.2% pass@1，规则基SFT达到34.1% pass@1，两者15.9个百分点的差距完全归因于能力上限和格式知识壁垒；10/20任务类型基础表现为0%，3/20类型需要精确临床代码且无法通过探索发现。

Conclusion: 提出了一个决策/格式知识/查询分类法来预测RL的可学习性，并给出了解决方案：SFT用于注入代码知识，RL用于学习条件判断逻辑。

Abstract: Clinical protocol-execution tasks -- checking a lab value, applying a threshold, placing a correctly structured FHIR order -- are natural candidates for RL from world feedback: once clinical SMEs encode decision logic into a verifier, that verifier grades unlimited rollouts without per-episode annotation. But applying RL requires a sound feedback channel and sufficient base capability. We audit MedAgentBench v1/v2, find a 41.7\% silent-finish ceiling that makes inaction the RL dominant strategy, and construct \textbf{MedAgentBench-v3 (MAB-v3)} (508 tasks, 8.9\% ceiling). Training Qwen3-8B exposes two structural barriers: a \emph{capability ceiling} (10/20 task types have 0\% base performance, zero gradient) and a \emph{format-knowledge barrier} (3/20 types require exact clinical codes undiscoverable by exploration). Pure RL reaches 18.2\% pass@1 vs.\ 34.1\% for rule-based SFT; the 15.9~pp gap is attributable entirely to these barriers. A decision/format-knowledge/lookup taxonomy predicts RL learnability and prescribes the fix: SFT to inject codes, RL to learn conditionals.

### [201] [Procedural Memory Distillation: Online Reflection for Self-Improving Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01480)
*Ye Liu,Srijan Bansal,Bo Pang,Yang Li,Zeyu Leo Liu,Yifei Ming,Zixuan Ke,Shafiq Joty,Semih Yavuz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出过程记忆蒸馏（PMD），通过跨回合、跨周期的轨迹信息构建三层抽象（原始轨迹、自反思策略、高阶行为模式）的可重用过程记忆，并利用记忆条件自教师机制将知识蒸馏回策略权重，在推理时无需额外记忆模块。在Qwen3-8B和OLMo3-Instruct-7B上，PMD相比SDPO在SCIKNOWEVAL和LIVECODEBENCH上分别提升3.8-5.5%和7.9-13.6%，且记忆与策略的协同进化是关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR及SDPO等方法仅利用回合级信号更新策略，忽视了rollout中丰富的过程信息，且跨回合、跨周期的信号（如哪些策略持续通过验证、哪些失败模式反复出现）无法被回合局部更新捕获。

Method: PMD构建三层抽象的过程记忆：原始轨迹、自反思策略与经验教训、跨问题的高阶行为模式，均从模型自身轨迹在线提取；记忆条件自教师利用累积经验监督学生在其自身rollout上学习，使学生将过程知识内化到参数中；核心设计原则是协同进化：策略生成rollout更新记忆，记忆塑造监督信号更新策略。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B和OLMo3-Instruct-7B上，PMD相比SDPO在SCIKNOWEVAL提升3.8-5.5%，在LIVECODEBENCH提升7.9-13.6%；消融实验表明冻结记忆或策略均导致性能下降超过10%，验证了协同进化的必要性。

Conclusion: PMD通过跨回合过程记忆的蒸馏有效提升了推理能力，协同进化的设计是实现性能提升的核心，且推理时无需额外记忆开销。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), along with recent selfdistillation variants such as SDPO, evaluates each rollout against a verifier and updates the policy from that episode-level signal. However, the richer procedural information in the rollout is rarely retained or reused. Across episodes and epochs, the model repeatedly encounters related problems under a changing policy, producing cross-episode signals that episode-local updates cannot capture: which strategies consistently pass verification, which failure modes persist, which patterns recur. We propose Procedural Memory Distillation (PMD), which converts these crossepisode signals into reusable procedural memory and distills it into the policy's weights during training. This memory functions as a training scaffold, absorbed into the policy itself, yielding a memory-free model at inference. PMD organizes the memory at three levels of abstraction: raw trajectories, self-reflected strategies and lessons, and higher-level behavioral patterns that recur across problems, all extracted online from the model's own trajectories. A memory-conditioned self-teacher draws on the accumulated experience to supervise the student on its own rollouts, enabling student to progressively internalize procedural knowledge within its parameters. The central design principle is co-evolution: the policy generates rollouts that update the memory, and memory shapes the supervision that updates the policy. Empirically, across Qwen3-8B and OLMo3-Instruct-7B, PMD improves over SDPO by 3.8-5.5% on SCIKNOWEVAL and 7.9-13.6% on LIVECODEBENCH. Co-evolution powers these gains: freezing either the memory or the policy trails PMD by more than 10% across SCIKNOWEVAL domains.

</details>


### [202] [The Agentic Garden of Forking Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01507)
*Jiacheng Miao,Jonathan K Pritchard,James Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现AI智能体通过设定不同角色，能够复现人类研究者在数据分析中的选择性报告问题（即不同分析路径导致不同结论），并提出了m值（multiverse value）和Agentic Bootstrap方法来量化分析路径的极端程度，从而评估科学证据的可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实证研究中不同分析选择常导致不同结论，但这些隐藏的分叉路径难以观察，缺乏系统性的量化评估方法。

Method: 让AI智能体扮演不同角色（persona）分析相同数据；在四个高 stakes 领域测试；引入m值（分析路径产生极端结果概率）和Agentic Bootstrap（用AI采样可行分析路径估计m值）。

Result: AI智能体复现了人类研究者72%的意识形态差距；86%的AI分析通过独立AI审查，78%通过人类专家审查；在人类移民研究中，13.5%的人类分析落在最极端5%的分析空间内（m<0.05）。

Conclusion: 科学证据不仅应评估单一报告分析，还应考虑其在所有合理分析分布中的位置；Agentic Bootstrap使该分布可观测，可作为科学可信度的判断标准。

Abstract: Empirical research rarely admits a unique analysis. Different analytical choices can lead to different conclusions from the same data, yet these hidden forking paths are difficult to observe. We show that AI agents capture much of the analytical variation among human researchers while making these paths explicit. Across four high-stakes domains, assigning different personas is sufficient for AI agents to report divergent, often opposing, conclusions from the same data and question, with findings systematically aligned with those beliefs. In a study in which 42 human research teams analyzed the same immigration dataset, AI agents reproduced 72% of the human ideological gap in reported effect estimates. Despite reaching opposing conclusions, it is difficult to identify clear issues in each analysis based on the final AI reports: 86% passed independent AI review and 78% passed majority human expert review. These findings suggest that the central challenge is often not flawed analyses, but selective exploration and reporting from a large space of methodologically defensible analyses. AI agents may amplify this longstanding problem by making such exploration inexpensive and scalable. To address this, we introduce the m-value (multiverse value), the probability that an analysis path would produce a claim at least as extreme as the reported one. We further introduce Agentic Bootstrap, which estimates the m-value by using AI agents to sample plausible analysis paths. Applied to the human immigration study, 13.5% of reported human analyses fell in the most extreme 5% of the analysis space (m<0.05). Scientific evidence should therefore be evaluated not only by a single reported analysis but also by its position within the distribution of analyses that could reasonably have been reported. Agentic Bootstrap makes this distribution observable and turns it into a criterion for scientific credibility.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: AI agents that autonomously execute tool calls on a user's behalf raise pressing questions about permission management: what role could users play, and what role should they play? Despite many proposed approaches, the user's role in agentic permission management remains under explored. We introduce Janus, a playground system for implementing and evaluating user-involved agentic permission management designs. Janus consists of two components: Janus-Core, a modular agentic system supporting a diverse spectrum of permission management designs, and Janus-Harness, an automated evaluation framework. Grounded in a conceptual model that identifies key design axes for user involvement, we implement six permission assistants spanning the design space and evaluate them across three scenarios and three synthetic responders. We demonstrate that user input is critical and can significantly strengthen privacy and security, that AI augmentation of user decisions can help reduce cognitive load, and that realistic user behavior including permission fatigue must be accounted for in system design. No single design performs optimally across all contexts, motivating a more principled and context-sensitive approach to deploying permission assistants in agentic systems. Janus is publicly available to support future investigation into this dimension of agentic system design.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Semi-CoT对每个未标注问题采样多个伪CoT，估计答案级语义熵，选择低熵推理链作为可靠的伪CoT示例，实现从推理时优化到半监督伪监督的扩展。

Result: 在AQuA、SVAMP、GSM8K和MultiArith上的实验表明，熵门控选择出高精度伪CoT（伪答案精度91.36%-100%）；SVAMP和GSM8K有微小提升，AQuA出现负迁移，MultiArith达到性能上限。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has emerged as an effective approach for activating latent reasoning capabilities in large language models. However, most existing CoT methods use reasoning chains mainly as inference-time prompts, while the generated reasoning traces are rarely reused as semi-supervised learning signals. In this report, we define \textbf{Semi-supervised Chain-of-Thought Learning} and propose \textbf{Semi-CoT}, a simple framework that uses unlabeled questions to construct pseudo reasoning supervision. Semi-CoT samples multiple pseudo-CoTs for each unlabeled question, estimates answer-level semantic entropy, and selects low-entropy reasoning chains as reliable pseudo-CoT demonstrations. This extends the self-training view of CoT from inference-time refinement to semi-supervised pseudo-supervision. Pilot experiments on AQuA, SVAMP, GSM8K, and MultiArith show that the entropy gate selects high-precision pseudo-CoTs, with pseudo-answer precision ranging from $91.36\%$ to $100\%$. Semi-CoT also gives small gains on SVAMP and GSM8K, while AQuA shows negative transfer and MultiArith reaches a ceiling. These results suggest that unlabeled questions can provide reliable pseudo reasoning signals, but their effective use still requires stronger demonstration selection or student training.

### [205] [OPINE-World: Programmatic World Modeling with Ontology-error-Prioritized Interactive Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01531)
*David Courtis,Wenhao Li,Scott Sanner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OPINE-World是一个基于LLM的智能体，通过在线交互学习面向对象的程序化世界模型。它结合了两个协同工作的代理（行动代理和合成代理），使用反例引导归纳合成和贝叶斯本体误差度量来引导探索。在ARC-AGI-3基准测试上，无需逐游戏训练就解决了20/25个游戏，达到了78.4的动作效率分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: OPINE-World采用双代理协作框架：行动代理在环境中执行动作，合成代理通过LLM生成程序化世界模型代码，并使用回放验证和基于模型的规划进行细化。引入贝叶斯本体误差度量（ontology error）来引导探索，量化对象类型假设的充分性。
